--- FILE: ./landing/app/explorer/page.tsx ---

"use client";

import React, { useEffect, useMemo, useRef, useState } from "react";
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from "framer-motion";
import Link from "next/link";
import {
  Activity,
  ArrowLeft,
  Cpu,
  GitBranch,
  Globe,
  Layers,
  Radio,
  Search,
  Zap,
} from "lucide-react";

// ── Types ──

type SignalStatus = "PROPAGATING" | "SYNTHESIZED";

interface MeshSignal {
  id: string;
  hash: string;
  domain: string;
  payloadBytes: number;
  path: string[];
  status: SignalStatus;
  createdAt: number;
  latencyMs: number;
}

interface Telemetry {
  sps: number;
  activeDomains: number;
  density: number;
  latency: number;
}

interface DomainLoad {
  domain: string;
  count: number;
  sps: number;
  load: number; // 0 - 100
}

// ── Constants ──

const DOMAINS = [
  "dex.fluid",
  "settle.core",
  "game.mesh",
  "identity.sov",
  "bridge.eth",
  "oracle.feed",
  "nft.market",
  "governance.dao",
];

const NODE_IDS = Array.from({ length: 24 }, (_, i) =>
  `Node_${String(i + 1).padStart(2, "0")}`
);

const STATUS_COLORS: Record<SignalStatus, string> = {
  PROPAGATING: "#00F5FF",
  SYNTHESIZED: "#9D00FF",
};

// ── Helpers ──

function generateHash(): string {
  const hex = Array.from({ length: 8 }, () =>
    Math.floor(Math.random() * 256)
      .toString(16)
      .padStart(2, "0")
  ).join("");
  return `sig_0x${hex}`;
}

function pick<T>(arr: T[]): T {
  return arr[Math.floor(Math.random() * arr.length)];
}

function clamp(n: number, min: number, max: number): number {
  return Math.max(min, Math.min(max, n));
}

function randomWalk(prev: number, step: number, min: number, max: number): number {
  const delta = (Math.random() - 0.5) * step;
  return clamp(prev + delta, min, max);
}

function generatePath(): string[] {
  const len = 2 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 4);
  const shuffled = [...NODE_IDS].sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);
  return shuffled.slice(0, len);
}

function createSignal(): MeshSignal {
  const domain = pick(DOMAINS);
  const path = generatePath();
  return {
    id: Math.random().toString(36).slice(2),
    hash: generateHash(),
    domain,
    payloadBytes: Math.floor(Math.random() * 4096) + 64,
    path,
    status: Math.random() > 0.35 ? "SYNTHESIZED" : "PROPAGATING",
    createdAt: Date.now(),
    latencyMs: Math.floor(Math.random() * 120) + 12,
  };
}

function formatHash(hash: string): string {
  if (hash.length <= 18) return hash;
  return `${hash.slice(0, 10)}...${hash.slice(-6)}`;
}

// ── Main Component ──

export default function FluidicMeshExplorer() {
  const [signals, setSignals] = useState<MeshSignal[]>(() =>
    Array.from({ length: 12 }, createSignal)
  );
  const [selectedId, setSelectedId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [filter, setFilter] = useState<"ALL" | SignalStatus>("ALL");
  const [search, setSearch] = useState("");
  const [telemetry, setTelemetry] = useState<Telemetry>({
    sps: 1.4,
    activeDomains: DOMAINS.length,
    density: 34.2,
    latency: 18.5,
  });

  const searchRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);

  // Signal simulation engine
  useEffect(() => {
    let timeoutId: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout>;

    const tick = () => {
      setSignals((prev) => {
        const next = [createSignal(), ...prev];
        if (next.length > 50) next.pop();

        // Gradually flip older PROPAGATING signals to SYNTHESIZED
        for (let i = 5; i < next.length; i++) {
          if (next[i].status === "PROPAGATING" && Math.random() > 0.85) {
            next[i] = { ...next[i], status: "SYNTHESIZED" };
          }
        }
        return next;
      });

      const delay = 600 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 300);
      timeoutId = setTimeout(tick, delay);
    };

    timeoutId = setTimeout(tick, 700);
    return () => clearTimeout(timeoutId);
  }, []);

  // Telemetry random-walk engine
  useEffect(() => {
    const interval = setInterval(() => {
      setTelemetry((prev) => ({
        sps: randomWalk(prev.sps, 0.4, 0.8, 8.5),
        activeDomains: DOMAINS.length,
        density: randomWalk(prev.density, 1.2, 12, 96),
        latency: randomWalk(prev.latency, 2.5, 8, 95),
      }));
    }, 900);
    return () => clearInterval(interval);
  }, []);

  // Keyboard shortcut: focus search
  useEffect(() => {
    const onKey = (e: KeyboardEvent) => {
      if ((e.metaKey || e.ctrlKey) && e.key.toLowerCase() === "k") {
        e.preventDefault();
        searchRef.current?.focus();
      }
    };
    window.addEventListener("keydown", onKey);
    return () => window.removeEventListener("keydown", onKey);
  }, []);

  const filteredSignals = useMemo(() => {
    const term = search.trim().toLowerCase();
    return signals.filter((sig) => {
      const matchesFilter = filter === "ALL" || sig.status === filter;
      const matchesSearch =
        !term ||
        sig.domain.toLowerCase().includes(term) ||
        sig.hash.toLowerCase().includes(term);
      return matchesFilter && matchesSearch;
    });
  }, [signals, filter, search]);

  const selectedSignal = useMemo(
    () => signals.find((s) => s.id === selectedId) || null,
    [signals, selectedId]
  );

  const domainLoads = useMemo(() => {
    const counts: Record<string, number> = {};
    for (const sig of signals) {
      counts[sig.domain] = (counts[sig.domain] || 0) + 1;
    }
    const max = Math.max(1, ...Object.values(counts));
    return DOMAINS.map((domain) => {
      const count = counts[domain] || 0;
      return {
        domain,
        count,
        sps: parseFloat(((count / signals.length) * telemetry.sps).toFixed(2)),
        load: Math.round((count / max) * 100),
      };
    }).sort((a, b) => b.count - a.count);
  }, [signals, telemetry.sps]);

  return (
    <div className="relative min-h-screen overflow-hidden bg-[#020205] font-mono text-[#F0F0F0]">
      <div className="grain" aria-hidden="true" />
      <div className="mesh-bg fixed inset-0 -z-10 opacity-30" />

      {/* Top bar */}
      <header className="sticky top-0 z-40 border-b border-neutral-800 bg-[#020205]/90 backdrop-blur-md">
        <div className="mx-auto flex h-14 max-w-[1920px] items-center justify-between px-4">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-4">
            <Link
              href="/"
              className="group flex items-center gap-2 text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-neutral-500 transition-colors hover:text-[#00F5FF]"
            >
              <div className="relative h-6 w-6 overflow-hidden">
                <img
                  src="/fluidic-logo.png"
                  alt="Fluidic"
                  className="h-full w-full object-contain transition-transform duration-500 group-hover:scale-110"
                />
              </div>
              Fluidic
            </Link>
            <div className="h-4 w-px bg-neutral-800" />
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.15em] text-[#00F5FF]">
              <Activity className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
              Mesh Explorer
            </div>
          </div>
          <div className="hidden items-center gap-6 text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-neutral-600 md:flex">
            <span>Live Stream</span>
            <span className="h-1.5 w-1.5 animate-pulse rounded-full bg-[#00F5FF]" />
            <span>{signals.length} Signals Buffered</span>
          </div>
        </div>
      </header>

      <main className="mx-auto grid max-w-[1920px] grid-cols-1 gap-4 p-4 lg:grid-cols-12">
        {/* Telemetry HUD */}
        <section className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 lg:col-span-12 lg:grid-cols-4">
          <TelemetryCard
            label="Signals / Second"
            value={telemetry.sps.toFixed(2)}
            unit="SPS"
            icon={<Zap className="h-4 w-4" />}
            accent="cyan"
          />
          <TelemetryCard
            label="Active Domains"
            value={String(telemetry.activeDomains)}
            unit="DOMAINS"
            icon={<Layers className="h-4 w-4" />}
            accent="violet"
          />
          <TelemetryCard
            label="Wave-Field Density"
            value={telemetry.density.toFixed(1)}
            unit="%"
            icon={<Globe className="h-4 w-4" />}
            accent="cyan"
          />
          <TelemetryCard
            label="Propagation Latency"
            value={telemetry.latency.toFixed(1)}
            unit="MS"
            icon={<Radio className="h-4 w-4" />}
            accent="violet"
          />
        </section>

        {/* Search + filters */}
        <section className="lg:col-span-12">
          <div className="flex flex-col gap-3 border border-neutral-800 bg-[#0a0a0f]/80 p-3 md:flex-row md:items-center">
            <div className="relative flex-1">
              <Search className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 h-3.5 w-3.5 -translate-y-1/2 text-neutral-600" />
              <input
                ref={searchRef}
                type="text"
                value={search}
                onChange={(e) => setSearch(e.target.value)}
                onKeyDown={(e) => {
                  if (e.key === "Enter") {
                    e.preventDefault();
                  }
                }}
                placeholder="domain or signal hash"
                className="w-full border border-neutral-800 bg-[#020205] py-2 pl-9 pr-4 text-[12px] text-[#F0F0F0] outline-none transition-all placeholder:text-neutral-700 focus:border-[#00F5FF]/50 focus:shadow-[0_0_15px_-5px_rgba(0,245,255,0.2)]"
              />
              <span className="pointer-events-none absolute right-3 top-1/2 hidden -translate-y-1/2 text-[10px] text-neutral-700 md:block">
                FLUIDIC:// SEARCH &gt;
              </span>
            </div>
            <div className="flex gap-2">
              {(["ALL", "PROPAGATING", "SYNTHESIZED"] as const).map((f) => (
                <button
                  key={f}
                  onClick={() => setFilter(f)}
                  className={`border px-3 py-2 text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.15em] transition-all ${
                    filter === f
                      ? "border-[#00F5FF] bg-[#00F5FF]/10 text-[#00F5FF]"
                      : "border-neutral-800 bg-[#0a0a0f] text-neutral-500 hover:border-neutral-600 hover:text-neutral-300"
                  }`}
                >
                  {f}
                </button>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        </section>

        {/* Signal feed matrix */}
        <section className="min-h-[520px] border border-neutral-800 bg-[#0a0a0f]/60 lg:col-span-7">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between border-b border-neutral-800 px-4 py-3">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-neutral-400">
              <GitBranch className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
              Live Signal Feed Matrix
            </div>
            <div className="text-[10px] text-neutral-600">
              Showing {filteredSignals.length} of {signals.length}
            </div>
          </div>
          <div className="max-h-[520px] overflow-auto">
            <table className="w-full text-left text-[11px]">
              <thead className="sticky top-0 z-10 bg-[#0a0a0f]">
                <tr className="border-b border-neutral-800 text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.15em] text-neutral-600">
                  <th className="px-4 py-2 font-normal">Status</th>
                  <th className="px-4 py-2 font-normal">Hash</th>
                  <th className="px-4 py-2 font-normal">Domain</th>
                  <th className="px-4 py-2 font-normal text-right">Payload</th>
                  <th className="px-4 py-2 font-normal text-right">Latency</th>
                </tr>
              </thead>
              <tbody>
                <AnimatePresence initial={false}>
                  {filteredSignals.map((sig) => (
                    <motion.tr
                      key={sig.id}
                      layout
                      initial={{ opacity: 0, x: -12 }}
                      animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
                      exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
                      transition={{ duration: 0.2 }}
                      onClick={() => setSelectedId(sig.id)}
                      className={`cursor-pointer border-b border-neutral-800/50 transition-colors ${
                        selectedId === sig.id
                          ? "bg-[#00F5FF]/8"
                          : "hover:bg-white/[0.02]"
                      }`}
                    >
                      <td className="px-4 py-2.5">
                        <span
                          className="inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wider"
                          style={{ color: STATUS_COLORS[sig.status] }}
                        >
                          <span
                            className="h-1.5 w-1.5 rounded-full"
                            style={{ backgroundColor: STATUS_COLORS[sig.status] }}
                          />
                          {sig.status}
                        </span>
                      </td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-2.5 font-mono text-neutral-300">
                        {formatHash(sig.hash)}
                      </td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-2.5 text-neutral-400">{sig.domain}</td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-2.5 text-right text-neutral-500">
                        {sig.payloadBytes} B
                      </td>
                      <td className="px-4 py-2.5 text-right text-neutral-500">
                        {sig.latencyMs}ms
                      </td>
                    </motion.tr>
                  ))}
                </AnimatePresence>
                {filteredSignals.length === 0 && (
                  <tr>
                    <td
                      colSpan={5}
                      className="px-4 py-12 text-center text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-neutral-600"
                    >
                      No signals match the current filter.
                    </td>
                  </tr>
                )}
              </tbody>
            </table>
          </div>
        </section>

        {/* Trace panel */}
        <section className="flex min-h-[520px] flex-col border border-neutral-800 bg-[#0a0a0f]/60 lg:col-span-5">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 border-b border-neutral-800 px-4 py-3 text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-neutral-400">
            <Cpu className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
            Interactive Trace Panel
          </div>
          <div className="flex flex-1 flex-col items-center justify-center p-4">
            {selectedSignal ? (
              <TraceVisualizer signal={selectedSignal} />
            ) : (
              <div className="text-center">
                <div className="mb-3 inline-flex h-12 w-12 items-center justify-center rounded-full border border-neutral-800 bg-[#020205]">
                  <GitBranch className="h-5 w-5 text-neutral-600" />
                </div>
                <p className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-neutral-600">
                  Select a signal to trace propagation
                </p>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </section>

        {/* Domain heatmap grid */}
        <section className="lg:col-span-12">
          <div className="mb-3 flex items-center gap-2 text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-neutral-400">
            <Layers className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
            Concurrency Domain Heatmap
          </div>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 md:grid-cols-4">
            {domainLoads.map((d) => (
              <DomainHeatmapCard key={d.domain} load={d} />
            ))}
          </div>
        </section>
      </main>
    </div>
  );
}

// ── Sub-Components ──

function TelemetryCard({
  label,
  value,
  unit,
  icon,
  accent,
}: {
  label: string;
  value: string;
  unit: string;
  icon: React.ReactNode;
  accent: "cyan" | "violet";
}) {
  const color = accent === "cyan" ? "#00F5FF" : "#9D00FF";
  return (
    <div className="group relative overflow-hidden border border-neutral-800 bg-[#0a0a0f]/80 p-4 transition-all hover:border-neutral-700">
      <div
        className="absolute inset-0 opacity-0 transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100"
        style={{ boxShadow: `inset 0 0 40px -20px ${color}` }}
      />
      <div className="relative flex items-start justify-between">
        <div>
          <div className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-neutral-600">{label}</div>
          <div className="mt-2 flex items-baseline gap-2">
            <span className="text-2xl font-light tracking-tight" style={{ color }}>
              {value}
            </span>
            <span className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-wider text-neutral-600">{unit}</span>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div className="text-neutral-700" style={{ color }}>
          {icon}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function TraceVisualizer({ signal }: { signal: MeshSignal }) {
  const path = signal.path;
  const nodeRadius = 18;
  const width = 360;
  const height = 240;
  const startX = 30;
  const endX = width - 30;
  const y = height / 2;
  const stepX = path.length > 1 ? (endX - startX) / (path.length - 1) : 0;

  const points = path.map((_, i) => ({
    x: startX + stepX * i,
    y,
  }));

  return (
    <div className="w-full">
      <div className="mb-4 flex items-center justify-between border-b border-neutral-800 pb-3">
        <div>
          <div className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-neutral-600">Signal</div>
          <div className="font-mono text-[12px] text-[#00F5FF]">{formatHash(signal.hash)}</div>
        </div>
        <div className="text-right">
          <div className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-neutral-600">Domain</div>
          <div className="font-mono text-[12px] text-neutral-300">{signal.domain}</div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="relative flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden border border-neutral-800 bg-[#020205]">
        <svg width={width} height={height} className="block">
          <defs>
            <linearGradient id="traceGradient" x1="0%" y1="0%" x2="100%" y2="0%">
              <stop offset="0%" stopColor="#00F5FF" stopOpacity="0.2" />
              <stop offset="50%" stopColor="#00F5FF" stopOpacity="0.8" />
              <stop offset="100%" stopColor="#9D00FF" stopOpacity="0.8" />
            </linearGradient>
          </defs>

          {/* Connecting lines */}
          {points.slice(0, -1).map((p, i) => (
            <g key={`line-${i}`}>
              <line
                x1={p.x}
                y1={p.y}
                x2={points[i + 1].x}
                y2={points[i + 1].y}
                stroke="#1f1f24"
                strokeWidth="2"
              />
              <motion.line
                x1={p.x}
                y1={p.y}
                x2={points[i + 1].x}
                y2={points[i + 1].y}
                stroke="url(#traceGradient)"
                strokeWidth="2"
                initial={{ pathLength: 0, opacity: 0 }}
                animate={{ pathLength: 1, opacity: 1 }}
                transition={{ duration: 0.6, delay: i * 0.25, ease: "easeInOut" }}
              />
            </g>
          ))}

          {/* Nodes */}
          {points.map((p, i) => (
            <g key={`node-${i}`}>
              <circle
                cx={p.x}
                cy={p.y}
                r={nodeRadius}
                fill="#0a0a0f"
                stroke={i === points.length - 1 ? "#9D00FF" : "#00F5FF"}
                strokeWidth="1.5"
              />
              <motion.circle
                cx={p.x}
                cy={p.y}
                r={nodeRadius}
                fill="transparent"
                stroke={i === points.length - 1 ? "#9D00FF" : "#00F5FF"}
                strokeWidth="1.5"
                initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.5 }}
                animate={{ opacity: [0.4, 0.8, 0.4], scale: [1, 1.15, 1] }}
                transition={{ duration: 1.5, delay: i * 0.25, repeat: Infinity }}
              />
              <text
                x={p.x}
                y={p.y + 4}
                textAnchor="middle"
                fill="#F0F0F0"
                fontSize="8"
                fontFamily="monospace"
              >
                {i + 1}
              </text>
              <text
                x={p.x}
                y={p.y + 36}
                textAnchor="middle"
                fill="#8a8a8a"
                fontSize="8"
                fontFamily="monospace"
              >
                {signal.path[i].replace("Node_", "N")}
              </text>
            </g>
          ))}

          {/* Packet animation */}
          {points.slice(0, -1).map((p, i) => (
            <motion.circle
              key={`packet-${i}`}
              r="4"
              fill="#00F5FF"
              filter="drop-shadow(0 0 4px #00F5FF)"
              initial={{ cx: p.x, cy: p.y, opacity: 0 }}
              animate={{ cx: points[i + 1].x, opacity: [0, 1, 1, 0] }}
              transition={{
                duration: 0.8,
                delay: i * 0.25,
                repeat: Infinity,
                repeatDelay: points.length * 0.25,
                ease: "linear",
              }}
            />
          ))}
        </svg>
      </div>

      <div className="mt-3 grid grid-cols-3 gap-2 text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.15em] text-neutral-600">
        <div>
          <span className="block text-neutral-500">Path Length</span>
          <span className="text-[#F0F0F0]">{path.length} hops</span>
        </div>
        <div>
          <span className="block text-neutral-500">Payload</span>
          <span className="text-[#F0F0F0]">{signal.payloadBytes} B</span>
        </div>
        <div>
          <span className="block text-neutral-500">Status</span>
          <span style={{ color: STATUS_COLORS[signal.status] }}>{signal.status}</span>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function DomainHeatmapCard({ load }: { load: DomainLoad }) {
  return (
    <div className="group relative overflow-hidden border border-neutral-800 bg-[#0a0a0f]/80 p-3 transition-all hover:border-neutral-700">
      <div className="relative z-10 flex items-center justify-between">
        <div>
          <div className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.15em] text-neutral-400">{load.domain}</div>
          <div className="mt-1 flex items-baseline gap-2">
            <span className="text-lg font-light text-[#00F5FF]">{load.count}</span>
            <span className="text-[10px] text-neutral-600">signals</span>
          </div>
          <div className="mt-1 text-[10px] text-neutral-600">
            {load.sps.toFixed(2)} SPS · load {load.load}%
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div className="absolute bottom-0 left-0 h-[2px] bg-gradient-to-r from-[#00F5FF] to-[#9D00FF] transition-all duration-500" style={{ width: `${load.load}%` }} />
      <div
        className="absolute inset-0 opacity-0 transition-opacity duration-500 group-hover:opacity-100"
        style={{ boxShadow: "inset 0 0 30px -15px rgba(0, 245, 255, 0.12)" }}
      />
    </div>
  );
}

--- FILE: ./landing/app/page.tsx ---

"use client";

import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from "react";
import Link from "next/link";
import { motion, useScroll, useTransform, useSpring, useMotionValue } from "framer-motion";

// ── Types ──
interface MousePos {
  x: number;
  y: number;
}

// ── Spring config for human-feel parallax ──
const springConfig = { stiffness: 60, damping: 20, mass: 0.8 };

export default function FluidicPage() {
  const [mouse, setMouse] = useState<MousePos>({ x: 0, y: 0 });
  const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      if (!containerRef.current) return;
      const rect = containerRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
      setMouse({
        x: (e.clientX - rect.left - rect.width / 2) / rect.width,
        y: (e.clientY - rect.top - rect.height / 2) / rect.height,
      });
    };
    window.addEventListener("mousemove", handleMove, { passive: true });
    return () => window.removeEventListener("mousemove", handleMove);
  }, []);

  return (
    <div ref={containerRef} className="relative min-h-screen bg-[#0D0D1F]">
      <GrainOverlay />
      <MeshBackground mouse={mouse} />
      <Navigation mouse={mouse} />

      <main className="relative z-10">
        <HeroSection mouse={mouse} />
        <ConvergenceField />
        <DeveloperTerminal />
        <OperatorProgram />
        <Footer />
      </main>
    </div>
  );
}

// ── Grain Overlay ──
function GrainOverlay() {
  return <div className="grain" aria-hidden="true" />;
}

// ── Live Mesh Background ──
function MeshBackground({ mouse }: { mouse: MousePos }) {
  const x = useSpring(useMotionValue(0), springConfig);
  const y = useSpring(useMotionValue(0), springConfig);

  useEffect(() => {
    x.set(mouse.x * 40);
    y.set(mouse.y * 40);
  }, [mouse, x, y]);

  return (
    <div className="pointer-events-none fixed inset-0 -z-20 overflow-hidden mesh-bg">
      <motion.svg
        style={{ x, y }}
        className="absolute -inset-[10%] h-[120%] w-[120%] opacity-[0.18]"
        viewBox="0 0 100 100"
        preserveAspectRatio="none"
      >
        <defs>
          <pattern id="warpMesh" width="10" height="10" patternUnits="userSpaceOnUse">
            <path
              d="M 10 0 L 0 0 0 10"
              fill="none"
              stroke="#00E6A7"
              strokeWidth="0.15"
              opacity="0.5"
            />
            <circle cx="5" cy="5" r="0.4" fill="#7700FF" opacity="0.6" />
          </pattern>
        </defs>
        <rect width="100%" height="100%" fill="url(#warpMesh)" />
      </motion.svg>

      {/* Floating orbs */}
      <motion.div
        animate={{
          x: [0, 30, -20, 0],
          y: [0, -40, 20, 0],
        }}
        transition={{ duration: 20, repeat: Infinity, ease: "easeInOut" }}
        className="absolute left-[10%] top-[15%] h-[50vh] w-[50vh] rounded-full bg-[#7700FF]/15 blur-[140px]"
      />
      <motion.div
        animate={{
          x: [0, -20, 30, 0],
          y: [0, 30, -30, 0],
        }}
        transition={{ duration: 18, repeat: Infinity, ease: "easeInOut" }}
        className="absolute bottom-[10%] right-[5%] h-[45vh] w-[45vh] rounded-full bg-[#00E6A7]/10 blur-[130px]"
      />
    </div>
  );
}

// ── Navigation ──
function Navigation({ mouse }: { mouse: MousePos }) {
  const x = useSpring(useMotionValue(0), springConfig);
  const y = useSpring(useMotionValue(0), springConfig);

  useEffect(() => {
    x.set(mouse.x * -8);
    y.set(mouse.y * -8);
  }, [mouse, x, y]);

  return (
    <motion.nav
      style={{ x, y }}
      className="fixed left-0 right-0 top-0 z-50 flex items-center justify-between px-6 py-5 mix-blend-difference"
    >
      <Link href="/" className="group flex items-center gap-3">
        <div className="relative h-8 w-8 overflow-hidden">
          <img
            src="/fluidic-logo.png"
            alt="Fluidic"
            className="h-full w-full object-contain transition-transform duration-500 group-hover:scale-110"
          />
          <div className="absolute inset-0 rounded-full shadow-[0_0_20px_-5px_rgba(0,230,167,0.4)] opacity-0 transition-opacity duration-500 group-hover:opacity-100" />
        </div>
        <span className="font-serif text-xl font-light tracking-tight text-[#F0F0F0]">
          Fluidic
        </span>
      </Link>
      <div className="hidden items-center gap-10 font-mono text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-[#8A8AA3] md:flex">
        <a href="#convergence" className="transition-colors hover:text-[#00E6A7]">Convergence</a>
        <a href="#sandbox" className="transition-colors hover:text-[#00E6A7]">Sandbox</a>
        <a href="#operator" className="transition-colors hover:text-[#00E6A7]">Operate</a>
        <Link href="/docs" className="transition-colors hover:text-[#00E6A7]">Docs</Link>
        <Link href="/explorer" className="border-b border-[#7700FF] pb-0.5 text-[#F0F0F0] transition-colors hover:border-[#00E6A7]">
          Explorer
        </Link>
      </div>
    </motion.nav>
  );
}

// ── Hero Section ──
function HeroSection({ mouse }: { mouse: MousePos }) {
  const { scrollYProgress } = useScroll();
  const heroY = useTransform(scrollYProgress, [0, 0.3], [0, 150]);

  return (
    <section className="relative flex min-h-screen flex-col justify-center overflow-hidden px-6 pt-20">
      <motion.div style={{ y: heroY }} className="relative mx-auto w-full max-w-[1600px]">
        {/* Small structural label */}
        <div className="mb-8 flex items-center gap-4 font-mono text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.3em] text-[#8A8AA3]">
          <span className="h-px w-12 bg-[#7700FF]" />
          <span>Protocol Genesis v0.9</span>
        </div>

        {/* Massive headline — asymmetric */}
        <div className="relative">
          <h1 className="max-w-[1100px] font-serif text-[clamp(48px,12vw,200px)] font-light leading-[0.85] tracking-[-0.04em] text-[#F0F0F0]">
            The Future of
            <br />
            <span className="relative inline-block">
              <span className="stroke-text">Infrastructure</span>
              <motion.span
                initial={{ scaleX: 0 }}
                animate={{ scaleX: 1 }}
                transition={{ duration: 1.2, delay: 0.6, ease: [0.22, 1, 0.36, 1] }}
                className="absolute -bottom-2 left-0 h-[2px] w-full origin-left bg-[#00E6A7]"
              />
            </span>
            <br />
            <span className="text-[#00E6A7]">is Not a Ledger.</span>
          </h1>

          {/* Floating vertical label */}
          <div className="absolute -right-4 top-0 hidden h-full flex-col items-center justify-center gap-4 lg:flex">
            <span
              className="font-mono text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.4em] text-[#8A8AA3]"
              style={{ writingMode: "vertical-rl" }}
            >
              Asynchronous // Parallel // Sovereign
            </span>
            <div className="h-24 w-px bg-[#7700FF]/40" />
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Subheadline — offset right */}
        <div className="mt-16 ml-auto max-w-xl lg:mr-[15%]">
          <p className="font-serif text-lg font-light leading-relaxed text-[#8A8AA3] md:text-xl">
            Blockchains queue transactions. Fluidic synthesizes signals. The first
            asynchronous, parallel mesh protocol. We scaled beyond the sequential
            block.
          </p>
        </div>

        {/* Marquee CTA strip */}
        <div className="group relative mt-20 -mx-6 cursor-pointer overflow-hidden border-y border-[#F0F0F0]/10 bg-[#0D0D1F]/50 py-5 backdrop-blur-sm">
          <div className="marquee-track flex whitespace-nowrap">
            {[...Array(4)].map((_, i) => (
              <span
                key={i}
                className="mx-8 font-mono text-[12px] uppercase tracking-[0.35em] text-[#F0F0F0]/80 transition-colors group-hover:text-[#00E6A7]"
              >
                Enter the Mesh → Launch Testnet → Read the Litepaper → Enter the Mesh →
              </span>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      </motion.div>
    </section>
  );
}

// ── Convergence Field ──
function ConvergenceField() {
  const ref = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const [isConverged, setIsConverged] = useState(false);
  const { scrollYProgress } = useScroll({
    target: ref,
    offset: ["start end", "center center"],
  });

  useEffect(() => {
    return scrollYProgress.on("change", (v) => {
      setIsConverged(v > 0.55);
    });
  }, [scrollYProgress]);

  const lineProgress = useTransform(scrollYProgress, [0, 0.7], [0, 1]);

  return (
    <section
      id="convergence"
      ref={ref}
      className="relative min-h-[120vh] px-6 py-32"
    >
      {/* Section label — tiny, brutal */}
      <div className="mx-auto mb-20 flex max-w-[1600px] items-end justify-between">
        <span className="font-mono text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.3em] text-[#7700FF]">
          [SECTION 02]
        </span>
        <h2 className="max-w-2xl text-right font-serif text-4xl font-light leading-[1.05] tracking-tight text-[#F0F0F0] md:text-6xl">
          The
          <br />
          <span className="text-[#00E6A7]">Convergence</span>
          <br />
          Field
        </h2>
      </div>

      {/* SVG Signal lines + data packets converging */}
      <div className="pointer-events-none absolute inset-0 -z-10 flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden">
        <svg
          className="h-full w-full"
          viewBox="0 0 1200 800"
          preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid slice"
        >
          <defs>
            <linearGradient id="signalGradient" x1="0%" y1="0%" x2="100%" y2="0%">
              <stop offset="0%" stopColor="#7700FF" stopOpacity="0" />
              <stop offset="50%" stopColor="#00E6A7" stopOpacity="1" />
              <stop offset="100%" stopColor="#7700FF" stopOpacity="0" />
            </linearGradient>
            <filter id="packetGlow" x="-100%" y="-100%" width="300%" height="300%">
              <feGaussianBlur stdDeviation="2.5" result="coloredBlur" />
              <feMerge>
                <feMergeNode in="coloredBlur" />
                <feMergeNode in="SourceGraphic" />
              </feMerge>
            </filter>
          </defs>

          {[
            { x1: 0, y1: 0, x2: 600, y2: 400, dur: 1.8 },
            { x1: 1200, y1: 0, x2: 600, y2: 400, dur: 2.1 },
            { x1: 0, y1: 800, x2: 600, y2: 400, dur: 1.9 },
            { x1: 1200, y1: 800, x2: 600, y2: 400, dur: 2.3 },
          ].map((line, i) => (
            <g key={i} opacity={isConverged ? 1 : 0} className="transition-opacity duration-700">
              <SignalLine x1={line.x1} y1={line.y1} x2={line.x2} y2={line.y2} progress={lineProgress} />
              <SignalPacket x1={line.x1} y1={line.y1} x2={line.x2} y2={line.y2} dur={line.dur} active={isConverged} delay={i * 0.2} />
            </g>
          ))}
        </svg>
      </div>

      {/* Central synthesis node */}
      <div className="relative mx-auto flex h-[500px] max-w-[1600px] items-center justify-center">
        <SynthesisNode active={isConverged} />
      </div>

      {/* Feature grid carved into page */}
      <motion.div
        initial={false}
        animate={isConverged ? { opacity: 1, y: 0 } : { opacity: 0, y: 60 }}
        transition={{ duration: 0.9, delay: 0.3, ease: [0.22, 1, 0.36, 1] }}
        className={`mx-auto mt-24 grid max-w-[1600px] gap-[1px] bg-[#F0F0F0]/10 md:grid-cols-3 ${
          isConverged ? "mask-revealed" : "mask-hidden"
        }`}
      >
        <FeatureCarve index="01" title="Asynchronous State Consensus" description="No leader. No block proposer. Causal DAG ordering lets independent operators synthesize state in parallel, resolving conflicts only where signals actually collide." />
        <FeatureCarve index="02" title="Horizontal Scalability" description="10x nodes ≈ 10x speed. Mesh partitions process independent wave-streams concurrently. The network widens, not chokes." />
        <FeatureCarve index="03" title="Native Metabolic Incentives" description="Value decays if it sits idle. Operators and liquidity providers are rewarded for continuous synthesis, not hoarded block space." />
      </motion.div>
    </section>
  );
}

function SignalLine({
  x1,
  y1,
  x2,
  y2,
  progress,
}: {
  x1: number;
  y1: number;
  x2: number;
  y2: number;
  progress: any;
}) {
  const length = Math.hypot(x2 - x1, y2 - y1) + 200;
  const offset = useTransform(progress, [0, 1], [length, 0]);

  return (
    <motion.line
      x1={x1}
      y1={y1}
      x2={x2}
      y2={y2}
      stroke="url(#signalGradient)"
      strokeWidth="1.5"
      strokeDasharray={length}
      style={{ strokeDashoffset: offset }}
      opacity={0.7}
    />
  );
}

function SignalPacket({
  x1,
  y1,
  x2,
  y2,
  dur,
  active,
  delay,
}: {
  x1: number;
  y1: number;
  x2: number;
  y2: number;
  dur: number;
  active: boolean;
  delay: number;
}) {
  const pathId = `packetPath-${x1}-${y1}-${x2}-${y2}`;

  if (!active) return null;

  return (
    <>
      <defs>
        <path id={pathId} d={`M ${x1} ${y1} L ${x2} ${y2}`} />
      </defs>
      <circle r="4" fill="#00E6A7" filter="url(#packetGlow)" opacity="0.9">
        <animateMotion
          dur={`${dur}s`}
          begin={`${delay}s`}
          repeatCount="indefinite"
          rotate="auto"
        >
          <mpath href={`#${pathId}`} />
        </animateMotion>
      </circle>
      <circle r="2" fill="#F0F0F0" opacity="0.8">
        <animateMotion
          dur={`${dur}s`}
          begin={`${delay + dur * 0.5}s`}
          repeatCount="indefinite"
          rotate="auto"
        >
          <mpath href={`#${pathId}`} />
        </animateMotion>
      </circle>
    </>
  );
}

function SynthesisNode({ active }: { active: boolean }) {
  return (
    <motion.div
      animate={active ? { scale: 1, opacity: 1 } : { scale: 0.5, opacity: 0.3 }}
      transition={{ duration: 0.8, ease: [0.22, 1, 0.36, 1] }}
      className="relative flex h-56 w-56 items-center justify-center"
    >
      <svg
        className="absolute inset-0 h-full w-full"
        viewBox="0 0 240 240"
      >
        <defs>
          <linearGradient id="ringCyan" x1="0%" y1="0%" x2="100%" y2="100%">
            <stop offset="0%" stopColor="#00E6A7" stopOpacity="0.1" />
            <stop offset="50%" stopColor="#00E6A7" stopOpacity="0.6" />
            <stop offset="100%" stopColor="#00E6A7" stopOpacity="0.1" />
          </linearGradient>
          <linearGradient id="ringViolet" x1="0%" y1="0%" x2="100%" y2="100%">
            <stop offset="0%" stopColor="#7700FF" stopOpacity="0.1" />
            <stop offset="50%" stopColor="#7700FF" stopOpacity="0.7" />
            <stop offset="100%" stopColor="#7700FF" stopOpacity="0.1" />
          </linearGradient>
          <radialGradient id="coreGlow" cx="50%" cy="50%" r="50%">
            <stop offset="0%" stopColor="#00E6A7" stopOpacity="0.25" />
            <stop offset="60%" stopColor="#7700FF" stopOpacity="0.1" />
            <stop offset="100%" stopColor="#0D0D1F" stopOpacity="0" />
          </radialGradient>
        </defs>

        {/* Outer dashed ring */}
        <motion.circle
          cx="120"
          cy="120"
          r="110"
          fill="none"
          stroke="url(#ringCyan)"
          strokeWidth="1"
          strokeDasharray="8 6"
          animate={active ? { rotate: 360 } : { rotate: 0 }}
          transition={{ duration: 20, repeat: Infinity, ease: "linear" }}
          style={{ transformOrigin: "120px 120px" }}
        />

        {/* Middle ring with hex pattern */}
        <motion.circle
          cx="120"
          cy="120"
          r="95"
          fill="none"
          stroke="url(#ringViolet)"
          strokeWidth="1.5"
          strokeDasharray="40 20"
          animate={active ? { rotate: -360 } : { rotate: 0 }}
          transition={{ duration: 15, repeat: Infinity, ease: "linear" }}
          style={{ transformOrigin: "120px 120px" }}
        />

        {/* Hexagon frame */}
        <motion.polygon
          points="120,55 176,87 176,153 120,185 64,153 64,87"
          fill="none"
          stroke="rgba(0, 230, 167, 0.15)"
          strokeWidth="1"
          animate={active ? { rotate: 360 } : { rotate: 0 }}
          transition={{ duration: 30, repeat: Infinity, ease: "linear" }}
          style={{ transformOrigin: "120px 120px" }}
        />

        {/* Core glow */}
        <circle cx="120" cy="120" r="70" fill="url(#coreGlow)">
          {active && (
            <animate
              attributeName="r"
              values="70;78;70"
              dur="2.5s"
              repeatCount="indefinite"
            />
          )}
        </circle>

        {/* Inner core */}
        <circle cx="120" cy="120" r="50" fill="rgba(13, 13, 31, 0.8)" stroke="rgba(0, 230, 167, 0.3)" strokeWidth="1" />

        {/* Waveform bars inside core */}
        {[...Array(7)].map((_, i) => {
          const x = 96 + i * 8;
          const baseH = 6 + (i % 3) * 6;
          return (
            <rect
              key={i}
              x={x}
              y={120 - baseH / 2}
              width="3"
              height={baseH}
              rx="1.5"
              fill="#00E6A7"
              opacity="0.7"
            >
              {active && (
                <animate
                  attributeName="height"
                  values={`${baseH};${baseH + 14};${baseH - 4};${baseH + 8};${baseH}`}
                  dur={`${1.2 + i * 0.15}s`}
                  repeatCount="indefinite"
                />
              )}
              {active && (
                <animate
                  attributeName="y"
                  values={`${120 - baseH / 2};${120 - (baseH + 14) / 2};${120 - (baseH - 4) / 2};${120 - (baseH + 8) / 2};${120 - baseH / 2}`}
                  dur={`${1.2 + i * 0.15}s`}
                  repeatCount="indefinite"
                />
              )}
            </rect>
          );
        })}

      </svg>

      {/* Label with arrow pointing to node */}
      <div className="absolute -right-[140px] top-1/2 hidden -translate-y-1/2 items-center gap-4 lg:flex">
        <svg width="60" height="20" viewBox="0 0 60 20" className="overflow-visible">
          <line x1="60" y1="10" x2="10" y2="10" stroke="#00E6A7" strokeWidth="1" opacity="0.6" />
          <polygon points="10,10 18,6 18,14" fill="#00E6A7" opacity="0.8" />
        </svg>
        <div className="font-mono text-[10px] uppercase leading-relaxed tracking-[0.25em] text-[#00E6A7]">
          <span className="block">Synthesis</span>
          <span className="block text-[#F0F0F0]/60">Node</span>
        </div>
      </div>

    </motion.div>
  );
}

function FeatureCarve({
  index,
  title,
  description,
}: {
  index: string;
  title: string;
  description: string;
}) {
  return (
    <div className="group relative bg-[#0D0D1F] p-8 transition-colors duration-500 hover:bg-[#15152B]">
      <span className="font-mono text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.3em] text-[#7700FF]">
        [{index}]
      </span>
      <h3 className="mt-6 font-serif text-2xl font-light leading-tight text-[#F0F0F0] md:text-3xl">
        {title}
      </h3>
      <p className="mt-4 font-mono text-[12px] leading-relaxed text-[#8A8AA3]">
        {description}
      </p>
      <div className="absolute bottom-0 left-0 h-[2px] w-0 bg-[#00E6A7] transition-all duration-500 group-hover:w-full" />
    </div>
  );
}

// ── Developer Terminal ──
function DeveloperTerminal() {
  const [isHovered, setIsHovered] = useState(false);
  const [typedLines, setTypedLines] = useState<string[]>([]);

  const codeLines = [
    "await Fluidic.SignalHandler({",
    "  domain: 'fintech'",
    "}).gossipParallel({",
    "  method: 'UPDATE_STATE',",
    "  vectorClock: true,",
    "  finalize: 'causal_dag'",
    "});",
  ];

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isHovered) {
      setTypedLines([]);
      return;
    }

    let currentLine = 0;
    let currentChar = 0;
    const interval = setInterval(() => {
      if (currentLine >= codeLines.length) {
        clearInterval(interval);
        return;
      }

      setTypedLines((prev) => {
        const line = codeLines[currentLine].slice(0, currentChar + 1);
        const next = [...prev];
        next[currentLine] = line;
        return next;
      });

      currentChar++;
      if (currentChar >= codeLines[currentLine].length) {
        currentLine++;
        currentChar = 0;
      }
    }, 45);

    return () => clearInterval(interval);
  }, [isHovered]);

  return (
    <section id="sandbox" className="relative px-6 py-32">
      <div className="mx-auto max-w-[1600px]">
        <div className="mb-16 flex flex-col gap-6 md:flex-row md:items-end md:justify-between">
          <div>
            <span className="font-mono text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.3em] text-[#7700FF]">
              [SECTION 03]
            </span>
            <h2 className="mt-4 font-serif text-5xl font-light leading-[0.95] tracking-tight text-[#F0F0F0] md:text-7xl">
              Proof
              <br />
              <span className="stroke-text">of Skill.</span>
            </h2>
          </div>
          <p className="max-w-md font-mono text-[12px] leading-relaxed text-[#8A8AA3]">
            Hover the terminal. The protocol types itself. No placeholder. This is
            the actual surface area of a Fluidic integration.
          </p>
        </div>

        <div
          onMouseEnter={() => setIsHovered(true)}
          onMouseLeave={() => setIsHovered(false)}
          className="group relative mx-auto max-w-4xl overflow-hidden rounded-sm border border-[#F0F0F0]/10 bg-[#0A0A14] shadow-[0_0_80px_-20px_rgba(0,230,167,0.15)]"
        >
          {/* CRT effects */}
          <div className="crt-overlay crt-flicker" />
          <div className="pointer-events-none absolute inset-0 bg-[radial-gradient(circle_at_center,transparent_60%,rgba(0,0,0,0.4)_100%)]" />

          {/* Terminal header */}
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between border-b border-[#F0F0F0]/10 bg-[#15152B] px-5 py-3">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
              <div className="h-2.5 w-2.5 rounded-full bg-[#7700FF]" />
              <div className="h-2.5 w-2.5 rounded-full bg-[#00E6A7]" />
              <div className="h-2.5 w-2.5 rounded-full bg-[#F0F0F0]/20" />
            </div>
            <span className="font-mono text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-[#8A8AA3]">
              fluidic-core@node-07
            </span>
          </div>

          {/* Terminal body */}
          <div className="relative min-h-[300px] p-6 font-mono text-[13px] leading-relaxed md:p-10 md:text-[15px]">
            <div className="text-[#8A8AA3]">
              <span className="text-[#00E6A7]">$</span> fluidic sdk init --mode parallel
            </div>
            <div className="mt-4 text-[#8A8AA3]">
              <span className="text-[#7700FF]">&gt;</span> connection established to mesh subnet 0x7a3
            </div>

            <div className="mt-6 text-[#F0F0F0]">
              {codeLines.map((line, i) => (
                <div key={i} className="min-h-[1.5em]">
                  <SyntaxLine line={typedLines[i] || ""} />
                  {typedLines[i]?.length === line.length && i === typedLines.length - 1 && (
                    <motion.span
                      animate={{ opacity: [1, 0, 1] }}
                      transition={{ duration: 0.8, repeat: Infinity }}
                      className="ml-0.5 inline-block h-[1em] w-[0.6em] translate-y-0.5 bg-[#00E6A7]"
                    />
                  )}
                </div>
              ))}
              {!isHovered && (
                <motion.span
                  animate={{ opacity: [1, 0, 1] }}
                  transition={{ duration: 0.8, repeat: Infinity }}
                  className="inline-block h-[1em] w-[0.6em] translate-y-0.5 bg-[#00E6A7]/50"
                />
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>
  );
}

function SyntaxLine({ line }: { line: string }) {
  // Very basic syntax coloring for display
  const parts = line.split(/("[^"]*"|\b(?:await|domain|method|vectorClock|finalize|true)\b|[{}().,:])/g);

  return (
    <>
      {parts.map((part, i) => {
        if (!part) return null;
        if (/^"[^"]*"$/.test(part)) return <span key={i} className="text-[#00E6A7]">{part}</span>;
        if (/^(await|true)$/.test(part)) return <span key={i} className="text-[#7700FF]">{part}</span>;
        if (/^(domain|method|vectorClock|finalize)$/.test(part)) return <span key={i} className="text-[#F0F0F0]">{part}</span>;
        if (/^[{}().,:]$/.test(part)) return <span key={i} className="text-[#8A8AA3]">{part}</span>;
        return <span key={i} className="text-[#F0F0F0]/90">{part}</span>;
      })}
    </>
  );
}

// ── Operator Program ──
function OperatorProgram() {
  const [count, setCount] = useState(12450);

  useEffect(() => {
    const interval = setInterval(() => {
      setCount((c) => {
        const jitter = Math.floor(Math.random() * 7) - 3;
        return Math.min(25000, Math.max(0, c + jitter));
      });
    }, 2200);
    return () => clearInterval(interval);
  }, []);

  return (
    <section id="operator" className="relative px-6 py-32">
      <div className="absolute inset-0 -z-10 bg-gradient-to-b from-transparent via-[#7700FF]/5 to-transparent" />

      <div className="mx-auto max-w-[1600px]">
        <div className="flex flex-col items-start gap-12 lg:flex-row lg:items-end lg:justify-between">
          <div>
            <span className="font-mono text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.3em] text-[#00E6A7]">
              [SECTION 04]
            </span>
            <h2 className="mt-6 font-serif text-5xl font-light leading-[0.9] tracking-tight text-[#F0F0F0] md:text-8xl lg:text-9xl">
              Activate a
              <br />
              <span className="stroke-text">Synthesizer</span>
              <br />
              Node.
            </h2>
          </div>

          <div className="flex flex-col gap-8 lg:items-end">
            <div className="text-right">
              <div className="font-mono text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.3em] text-[#8A8AA3]">
                Estimated Mesh Capacity
              </div>
              <div className="mt-2 font-mono text-3xl text-[#00E6A7] md:text-4xl">
                {count.toLocaleString()}
                <span className="text-[#8A8AA3]"> / 25,000</span>
              </div>
              <div className="mt-1 font-mono text-[10px] tracking-[0.2em] text-[#7700FF]">
                NODES ACTIVE // SYNCHRONIZING
              </div>
            </div>

            <button className="group relative overflow-hidden border border-[#00E6A7]/40 bg-[#00E6A7]/5 px-12 py-5 transition-all hover:border-[#00E6A7] hover:bg-[#00E6A7]/10 hover:shadow-[0_0_60px_-15px_rgba(0,230,167,0.4)]">
              <span className="relative z-10 flex items-center gap-4 font-mono text-[12px] uppercase tracking-[0.25em] text-[#00E6A7]">
                Initialize Node
                <span className="h-px w-8 bg-[#00E6A7] transition-all group-hover:w-12" />
              </span>
              <motion.div
                initial={{ x: "-100%" }}
                whileHover={{ x: "100%" }}
                transition={{ duration: 0.6 }}
                className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-transparent via-[#00E6A7]/10 to-transparent"
              />
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Tactical status bars */}
        <div className="mt-20 grid gap-4 border-t border-[#F0F0F0]/10 pt-12 md:grid-cols-4">
          {[
            { label: "Mesh Uptime", value: "99.997%" },
            { label: "Avg Synthesis Latency", value: "0.8ms" },
            { label: "Parallel Streams", value: "4,192" },
            { label: "Causal DAG Depth", value: "∞" },
          ].map((stat, i) => (
            <div key={i} className="border-l border-[#F0F0F0]/10 pl-5">
              <div className="font-mono text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-[#8A8AA3]">
                {stat.label}
              </div>
              <div className="mt-2 font-serif text-2xl text-[#F0F0F0]">{stat.value}</div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>
  );
}
